=

=

=

Array();

=

function

{

=
elementID;




}







function
ftRegisterEntireMessageElementID(elementID)




{






ftEntireMessageElementIDs[ftEntireMessageElementIDs.length]
=
elementID;

function
getTimeRemainingString(
hours,
minutes
)

{


var
hourString


=

(
hours
==
1
?
"hr"
:
"hrs"
);


var
minuteString
=

(
minutes

==
1
?
"min"
:
"mins"
);





if
(hours
==
0)
{






return
minutes
+
"
"
+
minuteString;




}




if
(minutes
==
0)
{






return
hours
+
"
"
+
hourString;




}


return
hours
+
"
"
+
hourString
+
"
"

+
minutes
+
"
"
+
minuteString;


return
hours
+
"
"
+
hourString
+
"

"
+
minutes
+
"
"
+
minuteString;
}








function
FT_displayCountdown(forceUpdate)




{






if
(!document.layers
&&
!document.all
&&
!document.getElementById)
{








return;






}







FT_showHtmlElement("ftShipString",
true,
"inline");







var
FT_remainSeconds
=
FT_givenSeconds
-
FT_actualSeconds;







if
(FT_remainSeconds
<
1)
{








FT_showEntireMessageElement(false);






}
	








var
FT_secondsPerDay
=
24
*
60
*
60;






var
FT_daysLong
=
FT_remainSeconds
/
FT_secondsPerDay;






var
FT_days
=
Math.floor(FT_daysLong);






var
FT_hoursLong
=
(FT_daysLong
-
FT_days)
*
24;






var
FT_hours
=
Math.floor(FT_hoursLong);






var
FT_minsLong
=
(FT_hoursLong
-
FT_hours)
*
60;






var
FT_mins
=
Math.floor(FT_minsLong);






var
FT_secsLong
=
(FT_minsLong
-
FT_mins)
*
60;






var
FT_secs
=
Math.floor(FT_secsLong);







if
(FT_days
>
0)
{








FT_hours
=
(FT_days
*
24)
+
FT_hours;






}







window.setTimeout("FT_getTime()",
1000);







var
ftCountdown
=
getTimeRemainingString(
FT_hours,
FT_mins
);







for
(var
i
=
0;
i
<
ftCountdownElementIDs.length;
i++)
{








var
countdownElement
=
document.getElementById(ftCountdownElementIDs[i]);








if
(countdownElement)
{










if
(FT_CurrentDisplayMin[i]
!=
FT_mins
||
forceUpdate
||
countdownElement.innerHTML
==
""
||
firstTimeUpdate)
{












countdownElement.innerHTML
=
ftCountdown;












FT_CurrentDisplayMin[i]
=
FT_mins;












firstTimeUpdate
=
false;










}








}






}




}







function

{






for
(var
i
=
0;

<

{








FT_showHtmlElement(ftEntireMessageElementIDs[i],

}




}







function
FT_showHtmlElement(elementID,
shouldShow,
displayStyle)




{






var
element
=
document.getElementById(
elementID
);






if
(element)
{








if
(shouldShow)
{










element.style.display
=
(displayStyle!=null)?displayStyle:"";








}
else
{










element.style.display
=
"none";








}






}




}







function
FT_getAndClearCutOffEpochSeconds()




{






var
ftCutOffEpochSecondsElementID
=
"ftCutOffEpochSeconds";






var
ftServerCurrentEpochSecondsElementID
=
"ftServerCurrentEpochSeconds";







if
(document.layers
||
document.all
||
document.getElementById)
{








if
(document.getElementById(
ftCutOffEpochSecondsElementID
))
{










var
cutOffEpochSeconds
=
document.getElementById(
ftCutOffEpochSecondsElementID
).innerHTML;











if
(cutOffEpochSeconds
!=
"")
{












document.getElementById(
ftCutOffEpochSecondsElementID
).innerHTML
=
"";













if
(clientServerTimeDrift
==
null
&&
document.getElementById(ftServerCurrentEpochSecondsElementID))
{














var
serverCurrentEpochSeconds
=
document.getElementById(
ftServerCurrentEpochSecondsElementID
).innerHTML
*
1;














clientServerTimeDrift
=
new
Date().getTime()/1000
-
serverCurrentEpochSeconds;












}













return
(clientServerTimeDrift
==
null
?
0
:
clientServerTimeDrift)
+
cutOffEpochSeconds
*
1;










}








}






}






return
0;




}







function
FT_getCountdown(secondsLeft)




{






var
FT_currentTime
=
new
Date();






var
FT_currentHours
=
FT_currentTime.getHours();






var
FT_currentMins
=
FT_currentTime.getMinutes();






var
FT_currentSecs
=
FT_currentTime.getSeconds();






FT_givenSeconds
=
FT_currentHours
*
3600
+
FT_currentMins
*
60
+
FT_currentSecs;






var
FT_secondsFromCat
=
146452;







if
(secondsLeft!=null)






	FT_secondsFromCat=secondsLeft;






FT_givenSeconds
+=
FT_secondsFromCat;






FT_getTime();




}







function
FT_getTime()




{






var
FT_newCurrentTime
=
new
Date();






var
FT_actualHours
=
FT_newCurrentTime.getHours();






var
FT_actualMins
=
FT_newCurrentTime.getMinutes();






var
FT_actualSecs
=
FT_newCurrentTime.getSeconds();






FT_actualSeconds
=
FT_actualHours
*
3600
+
FT_actualMins
*
60
+
FT_actualSecs;







var
cutOffTimeFromPageElement
=
FT_getAndClearCutOffEpochSeconds();






if
(cutOffTimeFromPageElement)
{








var
countDownSeconds
=
cutOffTimeFromPageElement
-
FT_newCurrentTime.getTime()/1000;








if
(countDownSeconds>=1)
{










FT_showEntireMessageElement(true);








}








FT_givenSeconds
=
countDownSeconds
+
FT_actualSeconds;






}







FT_displayCountdown();




}

onAjaxUpdate_fast_track(asin)




{

timerDiv
=
document.getElementById("ftMessageTimer");

cutOffElems
=
document.getElementsByName("promise-cutoff-time."+asin);







if
(cutOffElems
==
null
||
cutOffElems.length
==
0)
{








return;






}







if
(timerDiv
&&
timerDiv.style)
{








timerDiv.style.display
=
'inline';






}







var
cutOffTimeVal
=
cutOffElems[0].value;






var
cutOffTime
=
parseInt(cutOffTimeVal);






var
currSecs
=
new
Date().getTime()/1000;






var
secsLeft
=
cutOffTime
-
currSecs;
//countDown






FT_getCountdown(secsLeft);




}





FT_getCountdown();

<p
style="margin-top:
0;">Montreal
trio
Land
of
Talk,
spearheaded
by
vocalist
and
songwriter
Elizabeth
Powell,
have
released
their
sophomore
full-length
album,
Cloak
and
Cipher.
Joining
Powell
on
the
album
are
Eoin
O
Laoghaire
(bass)
and
Andrew
Barr
(drums)
and
special
guests
drawn
from
the
Montreal
music
scene
and
beyond
including
Patrick
Watson
as
well
as
members
of
Stars,
Silver
Mount
Zion
Band,
Wintersleep,
Besnard
...

class="readMore"
style="display:
inline"

more
in
Amazon's

<div
class="drkgry">












This
is
one
of
my
favorite
albums.
A
friend
got
me
into
this
band
a
few
months
ago,
and
I
ignored
them
until
the
song
All
My
Friends
came
up
on
my
shuffle.
I
was
obsessed
with
it,
and
hesitant
to
listen
to
the
other
six
songs
because
I
was
sure
that
they
could
not
be
as
good
as
the
one
I'd
already
heard.
That
was
not
the
case.











<br
/>











<br
/>Land
of
Talk
is
a
straight-up
garage
band,
but
with
enough
pop
influence
to
be
listenable
as
all
hell.
Doubling
as
the
frontwoman,
guitarist
Liz
Powell
gives
the
band
an
energy
that's
impossible
to
ignore.
Even
on
the
downtempo
tracks,
there's
a
gritty
sweetness
to
her
voice
that
captivates.
There's
no
way
to
describe
this
album
adequately
to
someone
who
hasn't
heard
it.
Get
it
as
soon
as
you
can.

{

voteAjaxDefaultBeforeSendReviews
=
function(buttonAnchor,

{




messageContainer.html('Sending

};

voteAjaxDefaultSuccessReviews
=
function(aData,
aStatus,
buttonAnchor,
buttonContainer,
messageContainer,
isNoButton,
inappUrl)
{





if
(aData.redirect
==
1)
{






return

(aData.error
==
1)
{

again');






messageContainer.hide();

==

<a

class="noTextDecoration"

#039;"
>please

messageContainer.find('a').attr('href',

}

}


};


var

=
function(aStatus,

function(){

=
this;






var

=
jQuery(this).parent();






var

=

for

change

'json',

},

});
